# Lizardmen Compendium

The ancient and inscrutable lizardmen dwell within their jungle cities, constructed in ages past and dedicated to a now crumbling world order. What remains of this civilization serves as a reminder of the primordial powers that once shaped the land, and the lizardmen make full use of the ancient power they still have at their disposal. This power ranges from ancient relics left over from their golden age to mighty dinosaurs used as beasts of burden and living weapons.

The lizardmen themselves come in several subspecies, each with a dedicated role to serve within the larger empire. All of these lizardmen regard outsiders with suspicion, if not outright hostility, and some will even form conquering armies determined to restore the old order. The players are most likely to encounter the lizardmen when exploring their jungle homes. The players may be attempting to traverse jungles, explore ruins, or acquire relics within the realm of the lizardmen, which will naturally lead to confrontations.



\columnbreak

 Alternatively, the lizardmen may be marching from their realm to impose their unfathomable will upon the world, which could lead to the players having to fend off their reptilian invasion.

This document provides content to help you run games that heavily feature the lizardmen or any of the primeval creatures that dwell in their realm. This content ranges from new spells used by the lizardmen, to rules for implementing the types of combat equipment they use, to a bestiary of the different types of lizardmen and the monsters they utilize. Whether the players only have a minor side quest featuring lizardmen or an entire campaign, any of the content here can be used to enhance your games.

<br>

### Art Credit
* Yurlok of Scorch Thrash - Jesper Ejsing, Wizards of the Coast

# Running Lizardmen Adventures
The setting you're running your adventures in will help determine the background of these lizardmen and their lore. They may be the primordial cousins of the lizardfolk in other settings, or they may be the stewards of an ancient empire. They may be noble protectors against ancient, long-forgotten evils or heartless conquers that eliminate other species without remorse.

Regardless of the specifics, there are some commonalities that tie lizardmen together, each of which could lead to conflict with the players:
* **Ancient:** Lizardmen are a primordial race, and their civilization is older than that of most mortals. This leads to them living in ancient cities and possessing powerful and valuable relics, which could put them at odds with treasure-hunting players.
* **Instructable:** Lizardmen possess a cold-blooded psychology that seems alien to most other races. They rarely display recognizable emotions and carry out their actions in a way that often seems callous to others. This behavior can often lead to conflicts with other races that the players could be pulled into.
* **Primal:** Despite lacking humanoid emotions, lizardmen are closely tied to their bestial natures and prone to bouts of primal aggression. This primal nature allows them to easily bond with other reptilian creatures, such as dinosaurs, which they often use in battle. Should the players wander into their territory, they may quickly find themselves on the receiving end of lizardmen’s primal aggression. 

\columnbreak



* **Devoted:** Despite their primal natures, lizardmen are prone to following orders from more powerful beings. They make for loyal and surprisingly orderly soldiers and will fight to the death for their cause. Should the players interfere with the plans of their masters, the lizardmen will show them no mercy.

### Lizardmen Motivations
The long-term motivations of the lizardmen almost always involve executing the great plan they believe their gods left for them to safeguard. This plan is meant to keep the world in order and guard against chaos. All other short-term goals are meant only to serve this greater plan. The only exceptions to this are when some of the lizardmen succumb to their more primeval natures and begin operating on base instinct. 

When role-playing lizardmen it’s usually best to keep their motivations both simple and difficult to read. When defending their territory or attacking those in possession of their relics, their motivations are as straightforward as a territorial animal’s. But when executing grand campaigns, they believe with further the great plan of their gods, their motivations may be indecipherable to outsiders. 

#### Common Lizardmen Motivations
* Destroy Intruders
* Protect or Reclaim Sacred Sites Artifacts
* Exterminate Members of Other Races Working Against the Great Plan (Whether They Know They Are Or Not)
* Collect Sacrifices for Their Ancient Gods
* Eliminate Otherworldly Forces of Chaos Entering the World
* Acquire Jungle Beasts for Labor and Wartime Use

<img
src='https://basiclandart.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/xln-276-forest-choi.jpg'
style='position:absolute;top:-80px;left:0px;width:820px;transform: scaleX(1)' />

 <img src='https://www.gmbinder.com/images/cPPYV7h.png' 
  style='position:absolute;right:-160px;top:75px;height:1400px;width:1416px;transform:rotate(180deg)' />

\pagebreakNum

## Lizardmen Tactics
Lizardmen are highly resilient and resourceful combatants who combine primal aggression with instinctive tactical acumen. While each subspecies and the various dinosaurs they make use of all fight differently, there are some general commonalities:

***Melee Oriented.*** Lizardmen usually have better melee options than ranged options. Skinks are exceptions to this, but for most other lizardmen and their dinosaurs, it’s usually best to close into melee range with the players as quickly as possible.

***Mixed Forces.*** Lizardmen forces generally benefit from mixing nimble skinks in with mightier saurian and dinosaurs. The skinks can debilitate foes while their kin move in for the kill.

***Rampaging.*** Most lizardmen, other than skinks, will begin rampaging when they drop to a third of their HP or less and other some other special circumstances. This condition forces them to engage their closest enemies in melee combat and can be used against them by cunning players. However, some lizardmen abilities boost their combat potential while they’re rampaging, so some lizardmen may intentionally drive themselves into a rampage.

#### Engagement
How the lizardmen engage in combat will largely depend on whether they have skinks among their forces. Skinks are master ambushers and will usually try to catch players by surprise and put them on the back foot before directing their harder-hitting allies to close in. 

### Running Lizardmen Encounters: Art Credit
* Ixalan Forest - Christine Choi, Wizards of the Coast
* Rootbound Crag - Grzegorz Rutkowski, Wizards of the Coast

\columnbreak

Lizardmen operating without skinks tend to be less stealthy and forgo the element of surprise to try to close in on the players as quickly as possible. That’s not to say they lack tactical nuance. Saurian warriors will still try to attack from optimal angles, surround foes, and pick off prime targets whenever possible.

#### Combat
In combat, lizardmen combine cold-blooded, brutal efficiency with primal ferocity. They execute orders they are given to a tee and are hyperfocused on their mission to the exclusion of almost all else. However, the targets of their wrath are subjected to animalistic brutality. When playing them, keep them focused on their objective and allow them to execute complex plans and make intelligent tactical decisions, but make sure any players they’re attacking feel like they’re being brutalized by an unrelenting beast.

#### Retreat
Lizardmen are utterly devoted to their cause, and most will fight to the death if it is in service to the great plan of their gods. This is not to say they are utterly unflappable. Skinks are skittish and may give in to their fear if the odds seem stacked heavily against them, causing them to scamper away from threats. Most other lizardmen struggle with the opposite instinct. When things start looking dire, they will enter a bloody rampage that leads to them fighting to the death, regardless of whether it's in the best interest of the lizardman force as a whole. 
Should the players retreat, most lizardmen will give chase if they have the strength to do so. They are remorseless and unforgiving by nature, and once they’ve marked prey for death, they rarely abandon their mission.


<img
src='https://i.ibb.co/ncCtjQJ/Rootbound-Crag-Ixalan-Mt-G-Art.jpg'
style='position:absolute;bottom:-120px;left:0px;width:850px;transform: scaleX(1)' />

 <img src='https://www.gmbinder.com/images/cPPYV7h.png'

# New Spells

## Lore of Beasts
This brand of magic draws on the power of the wilds and the animals that inhabit them. Those who practice it avoid civilization and live hermitic lives in the savage and untamed wilderness. Their magic harnesses the power of the beasts they dwell alongside, often by summoning wild spirits or unleashing the inner savagery of themselves and others to transform them into primeval creatures. The following spells are examples of the types of magic users of the Lore of Beasts often wield.

#### Amber Spear

*3rd-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:**  V S M (A Piece of Amber)
- **Duration:**  Instantaneous
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

You conjure a large amber hunting spear and launch it in a straight line at a point you can see within range. Upon reaching its destination or striking a solid surface, the spear shatters, producing an explosion within a 10-foot-radius sphere centered on that point. The spear can pass through spaces occupied by creatures and objects of large size or smaller. Each creature the spear moves through, as well as those within the explosion's radius, must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 6d6 piercing damage; on a successful one, the damage is halved.

***At Higher Levels.***  When casting this spell using a 4th-level spell slot or higher, the range increases by 20 feet and the damage by 1d6 for each slot level above 3rd.

\columnbreak

<br>

#### Aspect of the Beast

*4th-level  transmutation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
- **Range:** Touch
- **Components:**  V, S
- **Duration:**  Concentration, Up to 1 hour.
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

Upon touching a willing creature, you imbue it with bestial might. For the duration, the creature manifests a bestial weapon of your choice from the list below. When it takes the Attack action on its turn, it can make an additional attack with the bestial weapon as part of that action. The weapon is treated as a simple weapon with which the creature is proficient. Unless otherwise stated, it uses its Strength modifier for attack and damage rolls made with the weapon.

**Ripping Jaws.** The creature's mouth becomes filled with dagger-like teeth. Its jaws deal 2d8 piercing damage on a hit. If the bite damages a creature, the user gains temporary hit points equal to half the piercing damage dealt, which last until the spell ends.

**Tearing Claws.** The creature's hands transform into blade-like claws. These claws deal 2d6 slashing damage on a hit and count as finesse weapons. The creature can choose to replace any of its melee attacks made with the Attack action with its claws, including any off-hand attacks.

**Ramming Horns.** Gnarled horns grow from the creature's head. The horns deal 2d8 bludgeoning damage on a hit. If the creature moves at least 15 feet straight toward a target and then hits it with a horn attack, the attack deals an extra 2d8 bludgeoning damage, and if the target is Large or smaller, the creature can choose to push it up to 15 feet away.

 <img src='https://i.ibb.co/LN1X4rk/Shaman-of-Forgotten-Ways-Mt-G-Art-1024x750.png' style='position:absolute;right:-0px;top:-20px;width:820px;transform:scaleX(1)' />

<img src='https://www.gmbinder.com/images/cPPYV7h.png' 
style='position:absolute;right:-280px;top:95px;height:1400px;width:1416px;transform:rotate(190deg)' />

#### Bestial Spirit

*4th-level conjuration*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 40 feet
- **Components:**  V
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

A Large spectral beast appears at a location you choose within range. Though it appears substantial, it is intangible and can be passed through and occupied by other creatures.

Any hostile creature within 5 feet of the beast is so distracted by its presence that it has disadvantage on attack rolls. At the end of each of your turns, each hostile creature within 5 feet of the beast must make a Dexterity saving throw as the beast assaults it. The creature takes 4d8 force damage on a failed save, or half as much on a successful save. 

If a hostile creature moves more than 5 feet away from the beast, that creature must make the same saving throw against the beast's damage effect unless it took the Disengage action.

At the start of each of your turns, if no hostile creatures are within 5 feet of the beast, it moves up to 40 feet toward the closest hostile creature it can see. The beast has blindsight out to 120 feet and is blind beyond this range.


***At Higher Levels.***  When casting this spell using a 5th-level spell slot or higher, the beast's damage increases by 1d4 for each slot level above 4th.



\columnbreak

<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>

> ##### The Quickened Condition
> The following spell references the quickened condition. A quickened creature gains an additional action on each of its turns. That action can be used only to take the Attack (one weapon attack or unarmed strike only), Dash, Disengage, Hide, or Use an Object action. The *haste* spell applies the quickened condition among its other effects, and a creature cannot benefit from the quickened condition from multiple sources at once.

<br>

#### Call of the Pack

*5th-level enchantment*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Bonus Action
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:**  V
- **Duration:**  1 round
- **Classes:**   Ranger
___

Unleashing a primal howl, you stir the wild fervor within your allies. You and up to three other creatures you are aware of within range that can hear you are quickened until the start of your next turn. While quickened this way, these creatures gain advantage on attack rolls against any enemy if at least one of their allies is within 5 feet of that enemy and the ally isn't incapacitated.

#### Impenetrable Pelt

*5th-level  transmutation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1  action
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:**  V, S, M (a tuft of fur)
- **Duration:**  Concentration, Up to 1 hour
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

You weave magic to sheathe a willing creature you can see within range in a layer of tough fur and hide. For the spell's duration, any bludgeoning, piercing, or slashing damage the target takes is reduced by 5. This reduction applies before any resistances.

***At Higher Levels.***  When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 6th level or higher, the damage reduction increases by 1 for each slot level above 5th.

 <img src='https://i.ibb.co/2cTRzC2/Spirit-of-the-Aldergard-Kaldheim-Mt-G-Art.jpg' style='position:absolute;right:-50px;top:-90px;width:1100px;transform:scaleX(1)' />

style='position:absolute;right:-280px;top:105px;height:1400px;width:1416px;transform:rotate(170deg)' />

#### Monstrous Transformation

*6th-level transmutation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
- **Range:** Self
- **Components:**  V
- **Duration:**  Until dispelled
- **Classes:**   Druid, Sorcerer, Warlock
___

Drawing from wild energies, you transform into a mighty primal form of your choice: a **Feral Manticore**, a **Ravenous Hydra**, or a **Savage Dragon**. While transformed, you adopt the stat block of the selected beast (found later in this document). Your game statistics, including mental ability scores, are replaced by those of the chosen form, but you maintain your alignment and personality.

While in this new form:
* You assume its hit points.
* Your spell attack modifier and spell save DC replace its attack modifiers and saving throw DCs.
* If you're reduced to 0 hit points, you make death saving throws as usual. If you die, you revert to your true form.
* You can't speak, cast spells, or undertake any action requiring hands or speech.
* Your gear melds into your new form, rendering it inaccessible. As such, you can't activate, wield, or benefit from any of your equipment.

To attempt to end the spell, you may use your action to make a DC 15 saving throw using your original form's spellcasting ability modifier. On a successful save, the spell ends. However, if you fail this save three or more times within 8 hours, you must complete a long rest before attempting to end the spell again. A remove curse spell will also end the transformation.

If you take a long or short rest in your new form, only your new form gains the benefits of the rest

***At Higher Levels.***  When cast using a spell slot of 7th level or higher, the new form gains an additional 25 hit points for each slot level above 6th. If cast using a 9th-level slot, any features the new form can use only once per day can now be used three times per day.

\columnbreak

#### Primal Dominance

*2nd-level enchantment*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Components:**  V, S
- **Duration:**  10 minutes
- **Classes:**   Bard, Druid, Ranger
___

You emanate a commanding presence, compelling a primal creature to submit. Choose a beast, monstrosity, giant, dragon, or fey within range that can see and hear you. If the creature's Intelligence is 8 or higher, the spell has no effect. Otherwise, it must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failed save, it becomes charmed and frightened by you until the end of your next turn. Regardless of the save's outcome, you gain a +5 bonus to Charisma (Intimidation) and Wisdom (Animal Handling) checks when interacting with that creature until the spell concludes.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a 3rd-level spell slot or higher, you can target one additional creature for each slot level above 2nd.




#### Summon Flock

*1st-level conjuration*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** Self
- **Components:**  V, S, M (A worm or bug)
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 1 hour
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

Upon casting, you summon three crows that circle above you for the duration of the spell. As a bonus action, you can direct one of the crows to dive at a creature or object within 120 feet. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, it takes 2d4 piercing damage. If the attack is a critical hit, the target is blinded until the start of your next turn. Regardless of the outcome, the directed crow is expended. The spell ends if all crows are expended. For each crow circling above you, you gain a +1 bonus to Wisdom (Perception) checks.


***At Higher Levels.***  When you cast this spell using a 2nd-level spell slot or higher, you summon an additional crow for each slot level above 1st.

#### Wild Surge

*3rd-level transmutation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Components:**  V S M (a tuft of fur and a fang)
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 10 minutes
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

Select a willing creature within range to tap into its primal nature, transforming it into a bestial form. For the duration of the spell, the creature receives the following benefits:

<br>

* It gains 20 temporary hit points.
* It gains a +2 bonus to AC.
* It gains a +2 bonus to Strength saving throws and checks.
* It gains a +2 bonus to Wisdom (Perception) checks and Charisma (Intimidation) checks.
* When it hits with a melee weapon attack or unarmed strike, it deals one extra die of its damage.

***At Higher Levels.***  When casting this spell using a 4th-level spell slot or higher, the targeted creature gains an additional 5 temporary hit points for each slot level above 3rd.

>
> ***Regrow Spikes (1/Day).*** You regrow all of your spent spikes.

## Lore of Heavens
This brand of magic draws its power from the sky and the movements of celestial bodies. Those who study this lore often spend long periods of time observing the patterns and motions of the cosmos and are well known for their ability to discern events that have yet to pass through these observations. Spells from this lore also call upon the power of the skies, unleashing bolts of lightning, torrents of hail, or savage gusts of wind. The following spells are examples of the types of magic users of the Lore of Heavens often wield.

#### Comet's Call
*5th-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 300 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A piece of iron or nickel ore)
- **Duration:**   1 minute.
- **Classes:**  Wizard, Sorcerer
___

You channel the winds of magic to summon a comet from the heavens to the battlefield. You select a point you can see, 300 feet above you within range, causing a blue pulse to flash in the sky. 

At the start of each of your turns, roll a d6. On a roll of 1-3, nothing occurs. On a roll of 4-6, a 5-foot-radius comet materializes at the chosen point and immediately descends. The comet passes through any Large or smaller creatures and objects, exploding in a 30-foot-radius sphere when it hits a solid surface or a Huge or Gargantuan creature. The explosion's effects spread around corners. 

Each creature or object the comet comes in contact with, as well as those within the explosion's area, must make a Dexterity saving throw, taking the comet's full damage on a failed save, and half as much on a success. The comet's base damage is 5d8 fire damage plus 5d8 bludgeoning damage. Each time you roll to see if the comet appears and it doesn't, the fire and bludgeoning damage it deals each increase by 1d8. The spell ends after the comet lands.

\columnbreak

<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>



***At Higher Levels.*** Casting this spell using a 6th-level spell slot or higher increases either the fire damage or the bludgeoning damage (your choice) by 1d8 for every slot level above 5th.

#### Curse of the Midnight Wind
*3rd-level enchantment*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 150 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (Pinch of salt)
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**  Bard, Cleric, Warlock 
___

You summon a chilling wind, affecting an area within range that can be up to 40 feet long, 10 feet wide, and 10 feet tall. Up to six creatures of your choice within this area feel their fortune wane. Each targeted creature must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or be cursed by this spell for its duration.

While cursed:
* If the creature rolls an 18 or higher on an attack roll, ability check, or saving throw against an effect not caused by this spell, it automatically fails.
* When another creature makes an attack against the cursed target and rolls a 3 or lower on the attack roll, the attacking creature automatically hits.

At the end of its turn, an affected creature can attempt another Charisma saving throw, ending the curse's effect on it on a success.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, you can target one additional creature for each slot level above 3rd.

#### Lore of Heavens: Art Credit
* Meteor Swarm - Olivier Bernard, Wizards of the Coast
* Oracle's Insight - Raymond Swanland, Wizards of the Coast

#### Harmonic Convergence
*1st-level divination*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Components:** V S M (A piece of string)
- **Duration:** 1 round
- **Classes:**   Bard, Cleric, Druid
___

Divining auspicious omens, you grant a creature you <Br> can see within range a brief insight into the immediate <Br> future. Until the start of your next turn, if the chosen <Br> creature misses with an attack roll or fails a Dexterity <Br> saving throw, it can end the spell early to reroll the d20 <Br> and must use the new result. Similarly, when an attack <Br> roll is made against the chosen creature, it can end the <Br> spell early to force the attacker to reroll the d20, and the attacker must use the new result.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 2nd level or higher, you can target one additional creature for each slot level above 1st.

#### Ice Storm (Revised)
*4th-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 300 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (a pinch of dust and a few <br> drops of water)
- **Duration:**  1 Round
- **Classes:**  Druid, Sorcerer, Wizard
___

A barrage of rock-hard ice plummets from the sky, forming a 20-foot-radius, 40-foot-high cylinder centered on a point within range. The area becomes difficult terrain until the end of your next turn, and any  creature within it has disadvantage on ranged attack rolls.

When the ice storm initially appears or if a creature is inside its area at the end of your next turn, the creature must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, it takes 3d4 bludgeoning damage and 3d4 cold damage. On a successful save, it takes half as much damage.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 5th level or higher, both the bludgeoning and cold damage increase by 1d4 for each slot level above 4th.


#### Lighting Strike
*2nd-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A bit of fur and a rod of amber, crystal, or glass)
- **Duration:**  Instantaneous
- **Classes:**  Druid
___

You summon a bolt of lightning to strike a point you can see within range. Each creature within 5 feet of that point must make a Dexterity saving throw, taking 3d10 lightning damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or higher, you can summon an additional lightning bolt for each slot level above 2nd. These bolts can target the same or different points. If a creature is in the area of more than one lightning bolt, it is affected only once.

\columnbreak

<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>

#### Second Sight 
*2nd-level divination*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** Self
- **Components:** V S
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**   Bard, Cleric, Druid, Sorcerer, Wizard, Warlock
___

Guided by an astral prophecy, your sight extends beyond the present moment. Until the spell ends, when you or a creature within 30 feet of you makes an attack roll or a saving throw, you can end the spell prematurely, allowing the creature to roll an additional d20. This decision can be made after the original roll but before the outcome is determined. The creature then chooses which of the d20s to use for the attack roll or saving throw.

Alternatively, if an attack is made against you or a creature you can see within 30 feet of you, you can end the spell to roll a d20 and then decide whether the attack uses the attacker's roll or yours.

If multiple effects, such as another instance of this spell or a feature like the Lucky feat, attempt to modify a single roll, they negate each other, resulting in no additional dice being rolled.

#### Wind Blast
*3rd-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 90 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A legume seed)
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Classes:**  Druid, Sorcerer, Wizard
___

You summon a powerful gust of wind emanating from a 20-foot-radius sphere centered on a point within range and blasting out in the direction of your choice. Medium or smaller objects in this area that aren't secured and aren't being worn or carried are pushed up to 15 feet in the chosen direction. Each creature in the area must make a Strength saving throw. On a failed save, a creature is pushed in the chosen direction and knocked prone. The wind also disperses gas and vapor and extinguishes candles, torches, and similar unprotected flames in its area.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, the wind pushes creatures and objects an additional 5 feet for each slot level above 3rd.

## New Sload Mage-Priest Spells

### Lore of Beasts

#### Amber Spear
*3rd-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:**  V S M (A Piece of Amber)
- **Duration:**  Instantaneous
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

You conjure a large amber hunting spear and launch it in a straight line at a point you can see within range. Upon reaching its destination or striking a solid surface, the spear shatters, producing an explosion within a 10-foot-radius sphere centered on that point. The spear can pass through spaces occupied by creatures and objects of large size or smaller. Each creature the spear moves through, as well as those within the explosion's radius, must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 6d6 piercing damage; on a successful one, the damage is halved.

***At Higher Levels.***  When casting this spell using a 4th-level spell slot or higher, the range increases by 20 feet and the damage by 1d6 for each slot level above 3rd.

#### Bestial Spirit
*4th-level conjuration*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 40 feet
- **Components:**  V
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**   Druid, Ranger
___

A Large spectral beast appears at a location you choose within range. Though it appears substantial, it is intangible and can be passed through and occupied by other creatures.

Any hostile creature within 5 feet of the beast is so distracted by its presence that it has disadvantage on attack rolls. At the end of each of your turns, each hostile creature within 5 feet of the beast must make a Dexterity saving throw as the beast assaults it. The creature takes 4d8 force damage on a failed save, or half as much on a successful save. 

If a hostile creature moves more than 5 feet away from the beast, that creature must make the same saving throw against the beast's damage effect unless it took the Disengage action.

At the start of each of your turns, if no hostile creatures are within 5 feet of the beast, it moves up to 40 feet toward the closest hostile creature it can see. The beast has blindsight out to 120 feet and is blind beyond this range.


***At Higher Levels.***  When casting this spell using a 5th-level spell slot or higher, the beast's damage increases by 1d4 for each slot level above 4th.

\columnbreak

#### Summon Stampede
*9th-level Conjuration (Druid)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 90 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (a bit of cattle feed)
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 hour

You call forth a stampede of creatures that manifest in an unoccupied space you can see within range. These creatures use the Stampede stat block. The stampede disappears when it drops to 0 hit points or when the spell ends.

The stampede is an ally to you and your companions. In combat, the stampede shares your initiative count, but it takes its turn immediately after yours. It obeys your verbal commands (no action required by you). If you don’t issue any, it takes the Dodge action and uses its move to avoid danger.

#### Titanic Growth
*8th-level Transmutation (Druid)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (a seed)
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 hour

You cause a willing creature within range to tap into its primal essence, transforming into a colossal, bestial form. For the duration, the target gains the following benefits:
- The target’s size becomes Gargantuan (if it was smaller).
- If its Strength score is less than 19, it becomes 19 for the duration.
- It gains 50 temporary hit points for the duration of the spell.
- Its speed increases by 20 feet.
- It gains a +2 bonus to AC.
- It gains a +2 bonus to Strength checks and Strength saving throws.
- Its attacks with enlarged weapons or unarmed strikes deal an extra 2d8 damage on a hit.
 
#### Unleash the Beast
*7th-level Transmutation (Druid)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** Self
- **Components:** V
- **Duration:** 1 round

You unleash the primal beast within. Until the end of your turn, your speed increases by 30 feet and moving doesn’t provoke opportunity attacks, and you may make up to three melee spell attacks during the turn. You can make each attack at any point during your turn against a creature within 5 feet of you, targeting one or multiple creatures. On a hit, a target takes 4d10 Slashing damage and is knocked prone if it is your size or smaller.

***Using A Higher-Level Spell Slot.*** The damage of each attack is increases by 1d10 for every slot level above 7.

\pagebreakNum

### Lore of Death

#### Crippling Pain
*3rd-level necromancy*

- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 90 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A broken bone)
- **Duration:**  1 round
- **Classes:**  Cleric Warlock, Wizard

You cause a creature within you can see within range to be wracked with pain. The target must make a Constitution saving throw.

On a failed save, every time the creature takes a move, an action, a bonus action, or a reaction, before the start of your next turn, it takes 4d8 Necrotic damage.

On a successful save, it takes 2d8 Necrotic damage instead.

***Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot.*** You can target one additional creature for each spell slot level above 3rd.

#### Horrifying Laughter 
*6th-level enchantment*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (a tiny tart and a feather waved in the air)
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**  Bard, Wizard
___

You unleash a fit of deranged, magical laughter upon a creature you can see within range. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or suffer the following effects:
* Take 3d10 Force damage.
* Fall prone.
* Become Incapacitated and unable to stand for the duration.

On a successful save, the target takes half damage, and the spell ends immediately.

While the target remains under the spell's effect, any other creature that starts its turn within 30 feet of the laughing target and can hear it must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become Frightened of the laughing creature until the start of its next turn. You can choose any number of creatures you can see to be immune to this effect.

At the start of each of your turns, the target repeats the Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, it takes 3d10 Force damage again. On a success, the spell ends.

If the target is reduced to 0 hit points by this spell’s damage, it stabilizes but continues laughing, and can no longer attempt saving throws to end the spell. If the spell ends while the target has 0 hit points, it dies.

***Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot*** The initial and recurring Force damage increases by 1d10 for each slot level above 6th.

\columnbreak

####  Purple Sun
*9th-level transmutation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A pinch of lime, water, and earth)
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**  Sorcerer, Warlock, Wizard
___

You conjure a grim sphere of purple light at a point you designate within range. The sphere has a maximum radius of 60 feet and illuminates its area with dim light.

Any creature that either enters the sphere's area for the first time on its turn or begins its turn inside the sphere must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the creature is petrified for the duration. At the end of each of its turns, the target can make another Constitution saving throw. On a success, the spell ends on the target. However, if a creature accumulates three failed saves against this spell (including the initial failed save), it remains petrified indefinitely until the condition is cured by other means.

If a petrified creature is physically damaged or broken during this state, it will manifest the same damage upon being reverted to its original form.

### Lore of Fire

#### Burning Bolts
*6th-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 60 ft
- **Components:** V, S, M (A burnt stick)
- **Duration:** Instant
- **Classes:**  Sorcerer, Wizard

Choose up to three directions. A line of flames 120 feet long and 5 feet wide emanates from you in each direction you choose. Each creature in a line must make a Dexterity saving throw. A creature takes 8d8 fire damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one. A creature in the area of more than one line is affected only once.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 7th level or higher, you can create one additional line of flames for each slot level above 6th.

#### Meteor Swarm (Revised)
*9th-level Evocation (Sorcerer, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 1 mile
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:**  Instantaneous

You call down four blazing meteors at separate points you can see within range. Each meteor explodes in a 40-foot-radius sphere centered on its impact point. The spheres spread around corners.

Each creature in an affected area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 12d6 Fire damage and 12d6 Bludgeoning damage. On a successful save, the creature takes half as much damage. A creature caught in multiple areas of effect is only affected once.

The spell damages objects in the area and ignites flammable objects that aren’t being worn or carried.

\pagebreakNum

### Lore of Heavens

#### Lighting Strike
*2nd-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A bit of fur and a rod of amber, crystal, or glass)
- **Duration:**  Instantaneous
- **Classes:**  Druid
___

You summon a bolt of lightning to strike a point you can see within range. Each creature within 5 feet of that point must make a Dexterity saving throw, taking 3d10 lightning damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or higher, you can summon an additional lightning bolt for each slot level above 2nd. These bolts can target the same or different points. If a creature is in the area of more than one lightning bolt, it is affected only once.

#### Storm of Vengeance (Revised)
*9th-level Conjuration (Druid)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** Sight
- **Components:** V, S 
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 hour
___

A churning storm cloud forms, centered on a point you can see and spreading to a radius of 360 feet.  Lightning flashes in the area, thunder booms, and strong winds roar.  The cloud and an area stretching up to 5,000 feet beneath are affected in the following ways:

* When the creature enters the area for the first time on a turn or starts its turn there, it must make a Strength saving throw. On a failed save, it spend 4 feet of movement for every 1 foot it moves within the area until the start of its next turn. You choose for creature to ignore this effects  

* This area is Heavily Obscured to creatures other than you.  

* Ranged weapon attacks in this area are impossible unless you allow them.  

* If a creature starts its turn in the spell's area and is concentrating on a spell, the creature must make a successful Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC or lose concentration.  

* Gusts of strong wind (ranging from 20 to 50 miles per hour) automatically disperse fog, mists, and similar phenomena in the area, whether mundane or magical.

Additionally, At the start of each of your turns, you may choose one effcets from this options listed below to have happen that you have not already picked.

***Hail.***  Hailstones rain down from the cloud.  Each creature within its affected area must make a Dexterity saving throw.  The creature takes 4d6 Bludgeoning damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.  Objects in this area not being worn or carried automatically take 4d6 Bludgeoning damage.

\columnbreak

***Lightning.*** You call down 6 bolts of lightning from the cloud to strike 6 creatures or objects of your choice within its affected area.  Any given creature or object can't be struck by more than one bolt.  A struck creature must make a Dexterity saving throw.  The creature takes 10d8 Lightning damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.  Objects automatically take 10d8 Lightning damage.

***Rain.*** Acidic rain falls from the cloud.  Each creature and object within its affected area takes 3d4 Acid damage.

***Thunder.*** The cloud emits deafening blasts of thunder. Each creature within the affected area must make a Constitution saving throw.  On a failed save, a creature becomes Deafened for 1 minute and is Stunned until the end of your next turn. 

#### Wrath of the Four Winds
*8th-level Evocation (Druid, Sorcerer, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A small leaf)
- **Duration:** Instantaneous

You summon the might of the four winds to buffet your enemies. Choose up to four creatures within range. Each creature must make a Strength saving throw.

On a failed save, the creature is pushed up to 60 feet in a direction of your choice (you may choose a different direction for each creature). If it is pushed into a solid surface or into another creature that also failed its saving throw, the pushed creature takes 6d8 Bludgeoning damage, is knocked Prone, and is Dazed* until the end of your next turn.

If a pushed creature would collide with another creature that did not fail its saving throw, that second creature must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, both it and the pushed creature take 6d8 Bludgeoning damage, are knocked Prone, and become Dazed* until the end of your next turn. On a successful save, both take half damage and suffer no other effects.

On a successful Strength save, a creature is pushed up to 15 feet in a direction of your choice and suffers no further effects.

***Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot.***  The damage increases by 2d8 for every slot level above 8.

**New condition described at end of document*
 
### Lore of High Magic

#### Disruptive Pulse
*Evocation Cantrip (Sorcerer, Warlock, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:** Instantaneous

You unleash a wave of nullifying energy toward a creature within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 Thunder damage.

If the target is concentrating on a spell and must make a Constitution saving throw to maintain concentration as a result of this damage, you can choose to set the saving throw DC equal to your spell save DC instead of the normal DC.

***Cantrip Upgrade.*** The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

\pagebreakNum

#### Flames of the Phoenix
*7th-level Conjuration (Sorcerer, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Cction
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (an egg shell)
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute

You conjure a fiery phoenix that blazes across the battlefield. A phoenix made of flame appears in an unoccupied space of your choice within range and immediately moves up to 60 feet in a straight line, stopping early if it encounters an impassable barrier. The phoenix can pass through openings large enough for a Tiny creature.

At the end of its movement, the phoenix erupts in an explosion of magical fire. All creatures in its path, as well as those within a 15-foot radius of the point where it explodes, must make a Dexterity saving throw. A creature takes 7d8 Fire damage on a failed save, or half as much on a successful one.

After the explosion, the phoenix leaves behind a hovering ember at the point where it detonated. The ember remains for the duration of the spell.

***Reviving the Phoenix.*** As an action on your turn, you can command the ember to reconstitute into the phoenix. When you do, the phoenix reforms in the ember’s space, moves up to 60 feet in a straight line, and explodes again, repeating the effects above. The ember then returns to its new detonation point.

***Using A Higher-Level Spell Slot.*** The Fire damage increases by 2d8 for each slot level above 7th.

#### Power Word: Stun (Revised)
*8th-level Enchantment*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:** V
- **Duration:**   Instantaneous
- **Classes:**  Bard, Sorcerer, Warlock, Wizard
___

You speak a word of power that overwhelms the mind of one creature you can see within range. The target must make a Constitution saving throw. If the target has 150 hit points or fewer, it automatically fails.

* On a failed save, the creature is Stunned.
* On a successful save, the creature is Dazed*.

A creature Stunned or Dazed by this spell can repeat the Constitution saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success.

**New condition described at end of document*

\columnbreak

#### Rays of Magic
*6th-level Evocation (Sorcerer, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** Action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (prism glass)
- **Duration:** 1 round

You conjure three random rays of magic and hurl them at targets within range. Roll three times on the table below to determine the types of rays created. You can direct all the rays at one target or distribute them among multiple targets. Each ray requires a separate spell attack roll.

| d8 | Magic | Effect |
|:--:|:-----|:------|
| 1 | **Fire** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Fire damage and starts Burning*, taking 2d8 Fire damage at the end of each of its turns until the condition ends. |
| 2 | **Beasts** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Piercing damage. You or another willing creature within 60 feet of you can use its reaction to move up to half its speed toward or away from the target, without provoking opportunity attacks. |
| 3 | **Metal** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Bludgeoning damage, and its speed is halved as its limbs become heavy until the end of your next turn. |
| 4 | **Light** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Radiant damage, sheds bright light in a 5-foot radius, can’t benefit from being Invisible, and attack rolls against it have advantage until the end of your next turn. |
| 5 | **Life** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Slashing damage and is either pushed or pulled 20 feet in a straight line (your choice, toward or away from you). |
| 6 | **Heavens** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Lightning damage. You can choose a second creature within 10 feet of the target to take the same damage. |
| 7 | **Shadows** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Cold damage and deals only half damage with weapon attacks until the start of your next turn. A creature immune to Cold damage is unaffected by this secondary effect. |
| 8 | **Death** | On a hit, the target takes 3d10 Necrotic damage, and you gain temporary hit points equal to the damage dealt. These temporary hit points last for 1 hour. |

***Using A Higher-Level Spell Slot.*** You create one additional ray for slot level above 6.

**New condition described at end of document*

\pagebreakNum

#### Soul Quench
*3rd-level Necromancy (Cleric, Warlock)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V
- **Duration:** Instantaneous

You attempt to rip the soul from a creature you can see within range. The creature must succeed on a Charisma saving throw or become Incapacitated until the start of your next turn. While Incapacitated, it has a speed of 0. On a successful save, the target has Disadvantage on the next attack roll it makes until the start of your next turn. If a creature with 30 or fewer hit points fails the saving throw, it dies.

***Using A Higher-Level Spell Slot.*** A creature with 40 or fewer hit points will die; at 5th level, 50 hit points; at 6th, 60; at 7th, 70; at 8th, 80; at 9th, 90.

### Lore of Life

#### Gift of Life
*2nd-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 90 ft
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Classes:**  Artificer, Bard, Cleric, Druid, Paladin, Ranger

A creature you see with in range regains a number of hit points equal to 4d6 + your spellcasting ability modifier.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or higher, the healing increases by 2d6 for each slot level above 2nd.

#### Dwellers Below
*9th-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 100 ft
- **Components:** V, S, M
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**  Druid

Grasping limbs made of vines and branches sprout from the ground in a 30-foot square that is at least 10 feet deep, centered on a point within range. For the duration, these plants turn the ground in the area into difficult terrain. You can designate any number of creatures you can see to be unaffected by the spell.

**Grabbing Creatures With The Limbs.** When the limbs first appear, each creature of your choice that you can see within 60 feet of the spell's origin point must make a Dexterity or Strength saving throw (its choice) or take 10d6 bludgeoning damage and be pulled 30 feet toward the center of the area and become restrained. 

Subsequently, any creature that ends its turn in the spell's area or ends its turn restrained by the spell must also make this saving throw.

\columnbreak

**Being Restrained By The Limbs.** A creature restrained by this spell cannot use teleportation or interplanar travel. If damage from the spell reduces a target to 0 hit points while it is in the difficult terrain, the creature is pulled underground, and its body is destroyed along with everything it is wearing and carrying, leaving no trace except for magic items, which come to the surface after the spell ends. 

Any creature, including the restrained one, can use its action to free the restrained creature by succeeding on a Strength check against your spell save DC.


#### Regrowth
*6th-level necromancy*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
- **Range:** 60 ft
- **Components:** V S M (a diamond <br>worth at least 1,000 gp)
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Classes:**  Druid, Cleric

As you call out words of restoration, up to six <br> creatures of your choice that you can see within range <br> regain hit points equal to 3d6 + your spellcasting ability modifier. 

If you target a creature that has died within the last minute, that creature returns to life with 3d6 + your spellcasting ability modifier hit points. This spell can’t return to life a creature that has died of old age, nor can it restore any missing body parts.

Any creature targeted by the spell can immediately stand up without using any movement.

If you return one or more creatures to life with this spell, the diamond used to cast the spell is consumed.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 7th level or higher, the healing increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 6th.

#### Storm of Renewal
*8th-level Conjuration (Druid)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute

You summon a healing storm that takes the form of a raincloud in a 30-foot-radius, 10-foot-tall cylinder, centered on a point you can see within range directly above you. The cloud persists for the duration, releasing restorative rain that extinguishes exposed flames and washes away acid or slime covering the area.

When you cast the spell, and again at the start of each of your turns for the duration, you can choose up to three creatures within the cylinder. Each selected creature regains 4d8 hit points, and you can end one disease or one condition affecting it. The condition can be Blinded, Deafened, Paralyzed, or Poisoned.

### Lore of Light

#### Dazzling Light
*3rd-level evocation*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 120 fee
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:**   Instantaneous
- **Classes:**  Cleric, Bard

You unleash a burst of radiant light at a point you choose within range. Each creature in a 15-foot-radius sphere centered on that point must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or take 2d10 Radiant damage and become Blinded until the end of your next turn. A creature that succeeds on its saving throw takes half as much damage and isn’t Blinded.
 
***Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot.*** The damage increases by 1d10 for each slot level above 3rd.

#### Divine Judgment
*9th-level Divination (Cleric)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V
- **Duration:**  Instantaneous

You call down divine judgment upon those around you. Choose any number of creatures you can see within range. You gain insight into each creature's thoughts (if it has any), emotional state, and something that looms large in its mind—such as a fear, love, or hatred. You then choose for each creature to be subjected to one of the following effects:

**Guilty.**  The creature must make a Charisma saving throw (which it can choose to fail). On a failed save, the creature takes 8d6 Radiant damage, falls Prone, and is Stunned until the start of your next turn. If this damage reduces the creature to 0 hit points, it is disintegrated. A disintegrated creature and everything it is wearing or carrying, except magic items, is reduced to a pile of fine salt.

If the creature is a celestial, elemental, fey, or fiend, it is instead banished to its plane of origin (if it is not already there) and cannot return to your current plane for 24 hours by any means short of a *Wish* spell.

On a successful save, the creature takes half as much damage and suffers no other effects.

**Innocent.** The creature regains 8d6 hit points. In addition, it is cured of all diseases and any conditions causing it to be Blinded, Deafened, or Poisoned.

\columnbreak

### Lore of Metal

#### Final Transmutation
*9th-level Transmutation*

- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 60 ft
- **Components:** V, S, M (A bar of lead)
- **Duration:**  1 minute
- **Classes:**  Sorcerer, Warlock, Wizard
___

You speak a word of power that transforms a creature you can see within range. The target must make a Constitution saving throw. If the target has 150 hit points or fewer, it automatically fails. On a failed save, it is Petrified, turning to gold until the spell ends. On a successful save, the creature is Restrained until the end of your next turn.

**Ending The Effect.** A Petrified target can make a Constitution saving throw at the start of each of your turns, ending the effect on a success. However, if a creature accumulates three failed saves against this spell, it remains Petrified indefinitely until the condition is cured by other means.

**Effect On Other Creatures.** Any other creature that starts its turn within 60 feet of the petrified creature during the spell's duration must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become Obsessed* with the Petrified creature until the start of its next turn. You can choose any number of creatures you can see to be immune to this effect.

**Damaging A Petrified Creature.** If a Petrified creature is physically damaged or broken during this state, it will manifest the same damage upon being reverted to its original form.

**New condition described at end of document*

#### Plague of Rust
*3rd-level transmutation*

- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 60 ft
- **Components:** V, S, M (a piece of gold thread)
- **Duration:**  Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**  Artificer, Druid

You choose a creature with metal parts or a Medium or Small manufactured metal object weighing 80 pounds or less, such as a metal weapon, a suit of heavy or medium metal armor, or a metal door lock. A creature targeted by the spell can make a Constitution saving throw, ignoring the effects of the spell on a success.

An affected creature or object receives a -5 penalty to its AC, and any affected armor provides a -5 penalty to the AC it offers. Additionally, any weapon attacks made by an affected creature or using an affected object deal only half damage.

If you concentrate on this spell for the full duration, any nonmagical objects affected by the spell are destroyed, corroding into a pile of rust. A creature under the effects of the spell takes 3d6 necrotic damage at the end of each of its turns and makes a Constitution saving throw. The spell ends on the creature on a successful save.

\pagebreakNum

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, you can target one additional creature or object for each slot level above 3rd. The targets must be within 30 feet of each other when you target them.

#### Rebounding Blades 
*8th-level Conjuration (Bard, Cleric, Sorcerer, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 100 feet
- **Components:** V, S, M (A small magnet)
- **Duration:** 1 round

You conjure three spinning blades of returning and launch them outwards. Each blade appears in an unoccupied 5-foot cube adjacent to you and immediately flies up to 100 feet in a straight line in a direction of your choice. The blades hover at their destinations until the start of your next turn, at which point they move back toward you in straight lines. A blade disappears when it reaches you or after it has traveled a total of 100 feet.

The first time a blade enters a creature’s space (other than yours) during its initial flight or return, that creature must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, the creature takes 8d10 Slashing damage. On a successful save, it takes half as much damage.

***Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot.***  The damage increases by 2d10 for every slot level above 8.



#### Weapon of Power
*7th-level Conjuration (Bard, Cleric, Sorcerer, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 bonus action
- **Range:** 60 feet
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute

You conjure an animated weapon infused with magical power. Choose Bludgeoning, Piercing, or Slashing damage when you cast the spell. The weapon appears in an unoccupied space within range and lasts for the duration.

When the weapon appears, you may immediately make a melee spell attack against a creature within 5 feet of it. On a hit, the target takes 4d10 damage of the chosen type and suffers an additional effect based on the type selected:

* **Bludgeoning:** You can move the target up to 10 feet to an unoccupied space.

* **Piercing:** Treat any 1 or 2 rolled on the damage dice as a 3.

* **Slashing:** The target’s speed is reduced by 15 feet until the start of your next turn.

Until the spell ends, you can use a bonus action on each of your turns to move the weapon up to 20 feet to a space you can see and repeat the attack against the same or a different target within 5 feet.

***Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot.***  The damage increases by 1d10 for every slot level above 7.

### Lore of Shadow

#### Withering Resolve
*3rd-level enchantment*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 120 ft
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**  Bard
___

Choose a creature within range that can hear you. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw, or its mind becomes filled with crippling doubt and inner turmoil. On a failed save, for the duration of the spell, the target has disadvantage on all checks and saving throws not triggered by this spell, and attack rolls against it have advantage. At the end of each of its turns, the target can make another Wisdom saving throw, ending the effects on a success.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, you can target one additional creature for each slot level above 3rd.


#### Path of Shadows 
*7th-level Conjuration (Bard, Sorcerer, Warlock, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 Action
- **Range:** 30 feet
- **Components:** V
- **Duration:** Instantaneous

You summon swirling shadows to whisk away up to six willing creatures of your choice that you can see within range. Each creature is teleported to an unoccupied space you can see within 60 feet of you, and must appear within 15 feet of at least one other teleported creature.

Upon arriving, each creature becomes Invisible until the end of your next turn and may immediately take the Hide action (no action required).

#### Pit of Shadows
*6th-level abjuration*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 60 ft
- **Components:** V, S, M (A black cloth)
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute
- **Classes:**  Cleric, Sorcerer, Warlock, Wizard
___

You conjure a portal to a shadowy plane, opening a 20-foot square pit on an area of the ground you can see within range. Creatures within this area must make a Dexterity saving  throw. On a failed save, a creature is banished to a realm of darkness for the spell's duration. While in this realm, the creature is incapacitated.

At the end of each of its turns, the banished creature takes 3d8 psychic damage and must then make a Charisma saving throw. On a success, the spell ends for that creature. When the spell ends for a creature, it reappears in its original space or the nearest unoccupied space if its original space is occupied. If a creature dies while banished, its body remains in the shadow realm; however, any magical items it was wearing or carrying return to the original location.

***At Higher Levels.*** When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 7th level or higher, you can increase the pit's dimensions by 10 feet for each slot level above 6th.

\pagebreakNum

#### Weird (Revised)
*9th-level Illusion (Warlock, Wizard)*
___
- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 120 feet
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:** Concentration, up to 1 minute
___

You summon a sphere of pure nightmares that warps the minds of those caught within. When you cast this spell, you can designate any number of creatures you can see to be unaffected by it.

A 20-foot-radius sphere of nightmares appears, centered on a point of your choice within range. When a creature enters the sphere for the first time on a turn or starts its turn there, it takes 5d10 Psychic damage and must make a Wisdom saving throw. 

On a failed save, the creature drops whatever it is holding, loses concentration, and becomes Frightened of the sphere for the duration. While Frightened in this way, it can’t take reactions and must use the Dash action to move away from the sphere by the safest available route on each of its turns, unless there is nowhere to move. At the end of each of its turns, the Frightened creature takes 5d10 Psychic damage and can then repeat the Wisdom saving throw, ending the effect on itself on a success.

A creature that succeeds on its initial saving throw is immune to this spell for the rest of its duration.

On each of your subsequent turns, you can move the sphere up to 30 feet to a point you can see.

### Lord Mazhalmundi Spell

#### Eruption 
*8th-level evocation*

- **Casting Time:** 1 action
- **Range:** 150 ft
- **Components:** V, S
- **Duration:** Instantaneous
- **Classes:**   Druid, Wizard, Sorcerer

You choose a point you can see on the ground within range. The ground cracks and a burst of magma erupts in a 60-foot-radius, 120-foot-high cylinder centered on that point. Each creature in the affected area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 4d12 fire damage and 4d12 bludgeoning damage. On a successful save, it takes half as much damage.

Additionally, the ground in the area becomes superheated for 1 minute. The area becomes difficult terrain, and any creature that ends its turn in the area must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the creature takes 4d12 fire damage, or half as much on a successful save.

After the area cools down, it remains difficult terrain until cleared. Each 5-foot-square portion of the area requires at least 1 minute to clear by hand.

\columnbreak

> ##### New Condition: Burning
> The creature has been set ablaze by something that continues to damage it each round until it is extinguished. The default source described here is fire, but other sources could deal different types of damage, such as acid.
> * **Default Damage:** A burning creature takes 1d4 fire damage at the end of each of its turns unless the source that inflicted the condition states otherwise.
> * **Ending the Condition:** As an action, the burning creature can extinguish the fire by dropping prone and rolling on the ground. The fire also goes out if it is doused, submerged, or suffocated. For example, another creature could use an action to put out the flames with their cloak or by pouring water on them.
> * **Multiple Sources of Burning:** If a burning creature would gain this condition again from another source, the new burning effect only replaces the old if it deals more damage each round. Otherwise, it is ignored.

<br>

> ##### New Condition: Dazed 
> A dazed creature can’t take reactions and on its turn, it must choose whether it gets a move, an action, or a bonus action; it gets only one of the three.

<br>

> ##### New Condition: Obsessed 
> The creature becomes fixated on a creature or object, which becomes a source of its obsession. Being obsessed has the following effects on a creature:
> * While the creature can see a source of its obsession, it can't target any creature or object with an attack, spell, or ability except for a source of its obsession.
> * While the creature can see a source of its obsession, it can't cast spells or use abilities that target an area (such as the *fireball* spell) unless a source of its obsession is in that area. 
> *  The creature can't willingly move away from a source of its obsession.

\pagebreakNum

# Magic Items
The following are new lizardmen-themed magic items you can add to your adventures. They are both used by The Last Defender, and if players defeat him, you could give them the opportunity to loot these items for themselves. Otherwise, they could be treasures the players uncover while exploring ancient Lizardmen ruins and forgotten battlefields.


#### Spear of Dread Visions
*Weapon (spear), rare (requires attunement), 4,000gp*

This spear was said to have been wielded by the Old Ones themselves. Those struck by it are inflicted with visions of doom that sap them of their will to carry on. The spear grants a +1 bonus to attack and damage rolls made with it.

**Returning Throw:** If the spear is thrown, it immediately flies back to your hand after the attack.

**Visionary Assault:** Once during your turn, when you hit a creature with this weapon, you can inflict upon it a mystical vision. At the end of each of the affected creature's turns, it takes 2 (1d4) psychic damage for each vision it has been inflicted with.

A creature can have multiple visions simultaneously, and if it is suffering from three or more visions, it is blinded and has disadvantage on Intelligence, Charisma, and Wisdom saving throws and checks until the visions are removed.


Visions can be removed by the *remove curse* spell or any effect that can remove the blinded condition. A creature with visions or another creature within 5 feet can make a DC 15 Wisdom (Insight) check as an action, ending all visions on a success.

A creature with Truesight cannot gain these <Br> visions, and all visions are removed if a creature <Br> gains Truesight. 

\columnbreak

#### Hand of Gods
*Wonderous item, rare (requires attunement), 5,000gp*

This divine relic appears to be a golden gauntlet with an extended arm piece. While wearing it, its user can create blazing balls of sunlight in the gauntlet's palm, which can then be blasted at enemies.

To attune to this item, you must affix it to your arm, either at the wrist, elbow, or shoulder. Upon doing so, the prosthetic magically transforms, replicating the appearance and function of the limb it's replacing. Once attached, it becomes an integral part of your body.

**Radiant Assault:** Once per turn, when you would normally make an unarmed strike, you can instead opt to make a ranged spell attack with a range of 100ft. using this item. For this attack, add your Wisdom modifier and proficiency bonus to the attack roll. On a hit, the target suffers 4d10 radiant damage.

### Magic Items: Art Credit
* Spear of Heliod - Yeong-Hao Han, Wizards of the Coast
